  <script>
    (function() {
      /* Fix for framer-L6dd2 blur animation that uses targets-based scroll trigger
         (which relies on Lenis and breaks in static export). We use IntersectionObserver instead. */
      function initBlurFix() {
        var el = document.querySelector('#about-us-text .framer-17o6zsh');
        if (!el) return;
        /* If React already animated it away, nothing to do */
        if (!el.style.filter || el.style.filter === 'blur(0px)') return;
        var observer = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
          entries.forEach(function(entry) {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
              /* Animate blur out â€” match Framer's spring feel */
              el.style.transition = 'filter 0.7s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1), opacity 0.7s cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)';
              el.style.filter = 'blur(0px)';
              el.style.webkitFilter = 'blur(0px)';
              observer.disconnect();
            }
          });
        }, {
          threshold: 0.5,
          rootMargin: '0px 0px -15% 0px'
        });
        observer.observe(el);
      }
      /* Wait for React hydration to complete before checking */
      if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
          setTimeout(initBlurFix, 800);
        });
      } else {
        setTimeout(initBlurFix, 800);
      }
    })();
  </script>

  <script>
    (function() {
      // zmeczona styled directly in HTML

      // Carousel: always infinite — prevent pause/cancel, restart fast if stopped
      var _carouselAnim = null;

      function getUl() {
        return document.querySelector('.framer-pLjlU section ul, .framer-1lrgd3f-container ul');
      }

      function startCarousel(ul) {
        var V = Math.abs(parseInt(ul.style.left || '-2394', 10)) || 2394;
        _carouselAnim = ul.animate(
          { transform: ['translateX(0px)', 'translateX(-' + V + 'px)'] },
          { duration: V / 25 * 1000, iterations: Infinity, easing: 'linear' }
        );
      }

      function ensureRunning() {
        var ul = getUl();
        if (!ul) return;
        var ok = _carouselAnim &&
                 _carouselAnim.effect &&
                 _carouselAnim.effect.target === ul &&
                 _carouselAnim.playState === 'running';
        if (!ok) startCarousel(ul);
      }

      // Start immediately, then poll every 250ms to catch any interruptions
      ensureRunning();
      setInterval(ensureRunning, 250);
      document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
        if (!document.hidden) ensureRunning();
      });

      // Prevent Framer from pausing our carousel animation (e.g. on hover)
      var _origPause = Animation.prototype.pause;
      Animation.prototype.pause = function() {
        if (_carouselAnim && this === _carouselAnim) return;
        return _origPause.call(this);
      };

      // Prevent Framer from canceling our carousel animation
      var _origCancel = Animation.prototype.cancel;
      Animation.prototype.cancel = function() {
        if (_carouselAnim && this === _carouselAnim) return;
        return _origCancel.call(this);
      };
    })();
  </script>
  <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
      // ===== CURSOR DOT - dot is in HTML, JS only drives position =====
      var dot = document.getElementById('br-cursor-dot');
      var cx = 0,
        cy = 0,
        dotVisible = false;
      // Framer spring exact params: stiffness:1000, damping:60, mass:1 (transition4 from source)
      var sx = 0,
        sy = 0,
        vx = 0,
        vy = 0,
        lastTickTime = null;

      function tick(ts) {
        var dt = lastTickTime !== null ? Math.min((ts - lastTickTime) / 1000, 1 / 30) : 0;
        lastTickTime = ts;
        if (dt > 0) {
          vx += (320 * (cx - sx) - 34 * vx) * dt;
          vy += (320 * (cy - sy) - 34 * vy) * dt;
          sx += vx * dt;
          sy += vy * dt;
          // snap when very close â€” eliminates spring crawl near cursor
          var ddx = cx - sx,
            ddy = cy - sy;
          if (ddx * ddx + ddy * ddy < 2.25 && vx * vx + vy * vy < 25) {
            sx = cx;
            sy = cy;
            vx = 0;
            vy = 0;
          }
        }
        dot.style.transform = 'translate(' + sx + 'px,' + sy + 'px) translate(-50%,-50%)';
        requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }
      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      window.addEventListener('pointermove', function(e) {
        cx = e.clientX;
        cy = e.clientY;
        if (!dotVisible) {
          sx = cx;
          sy = cy;
          vx = 0;
          vy = 0;
          dot.style.opacity = '1';
          dotVisible = true;
        }
      });
      document.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
        dot.style.opacity = '0';
      });
      document.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
        if (dotVisible) dot.style.opacity = '1';
      });
      // Hover effect for links/buttons (generic)
      document.addEventListener('pointerover', function(e) {
        if (e.target && e.target.closest('a,button')) {
          dot.style.width = '24px';
          dot.style.height = '24px';
        }
      });
      document.addEventListener('pointerout', function(e) {
        if (e.target && e.target.closest('a,button')) {
          dot.style.width = '16px';
          dot.style.height = '16px';
        }
      });
      // ===== AUTO-SCROLLING TICKERS =====
      function initTicker(containerEl) {
        if (!containerEl) return;
        var ul = containerEl.querySelector('ul');
        if (!ul) return;
        var items = Array.from(ul.querySelectorAll('li')).filter(function(li) {
          return !li.hasAttribute('aria-hidden');
        });
        if (!items.length) return;
        var itemWidth = parseInt(items[0].style.width) || 380;
        var gap = 24;
        var setWidth = items.length * (itemWidth + gap); // width of one full set
        // Clone items for seamless infinite loop
        items.forEach(function(li) {
          ul.appendChild(li.cloneNode(true));
        });
        // Override SSR width:100% so ul can extend beyond the container
        ul.style.width = (setWidth * 2) + 'px';
        ul.style.maxWidth = 'none';
        ul.style.transition = 'none';
        ul.style.transform = 'translateX(0px)';
        var offset = 0;
        var speed = 50; // px/second
        var lastTime = null;
        var paused = false;

        function tick(timestamp) {
          if (lastTime !== null && !paused) {
            offset += speed * (timestamp - lastTime) / 1000;
            if (offset >= setWidth) offset -= setWidth;
            ul.style.transform = 'translateX(-' + offset + 'px)';
          }
          lastTime = timestamp;
          requestAnimationFrame(tick);
        }
        requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }
      initTicker(document.querySelector('.framer-1qp0mx6-container'));
      initTicker(document.querySelector('.framer-139atic-container'));
      // ===== LOTTIE ANIMATIONS â€” 3-step process section =====
      function initLotties() {
        if (typeof lottie === 'undefined') return;
        [{
          sel: '.framer-88ev2s-container',
          src: 'https://framerusercontent.com/assets/4ZemShxv5iWvazoEpKf4JxeXXrA.json'
        }, {
          sel: '.framer-b5a463-container',
          src: 'https://framerusercontent.com/assets/APttkivVfDAKfeXuGwWB5wFkDQ.json'
        }, {
          sel: '.framer-1sk53e8-container',
          src: 'https://framerusercontent.com/assets/BbQ693hcjJKH3cdv7UYJCZ6Lcs4.json'
        }].forEach(function(item) {
          var el = document.querySelector(item.sel);
          if (!el) return;
          el.innerHTML = '';
          var anim = lottie.loadAnimation({
            container: el,
            renderer: 'svg',
            loop: true,
            autoplay: true,
            path: item.src
          });
          anim.addEventListener('DOMLoaded', function() {
            el.querySelectorAll('.secondary').forEach(function(s) {
              s.setAttribute('stroke', 'rgb(255,117,31)');
            });
          });
        });
      }
      // lottie-web is loaded with defer, so it might not be ready at DOMContentLoaded;
      // poll briefly until available
      var lottieAttempts = 0;
      var lottieInterval = setInterval(function() {
        if (typeof lottie !== 'undefined') {
          clearInterval(lottieInterval);
          initLotties();
        } else if (++lottieAttempts > 30) {
          clearInterval(lottieInterval); // give up after 3s
        }
      }, 100);
      // ===== FIX: IFRAME SCROLL HIJACKING =====
      // iframe captures wheel events when hovered → page scroll freezes with Lenis.
      // Default: pointer-events off. On click inside wrapper: enable interaction.
      // On mouse leave: disable again so scroll works immediately.
      (function() {
        document.querySelectorAll('iframe').forEach(function(iframe) {
          iframe.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
          var wrapper = iframe.parentElement;
          if (wrapper) {
            wrapper.addEventListener('click', function() {
              iframe.style.pointerEvents = 'auto';
            });
            wrapper.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
              iframe.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
            });
          }
        });
      })();
    });
  </script>
</head>

        <script>
          /* Hero appear animation — word-by-word blur+fade (matches Framer template) */
          (function() {
            var ease = 'cubic-bezier(0.16,1,0.3,1)';
            var dur = '1.3s';

            /* Set initial hidden state on each word span, then stagger-animate to final */
            function animateWords(parentSel, startDelay, stagger) {
              var parent = document.querySelector(parentSel);
              if (!parent) return;
              var spans = parent.querySelectorAll('span');
              spans.forEach(function(span, i) {
                /* Initial state — set synchronously before first paint */
                span.style.opacity = '0';
                span.style.filter = 'blur(10px)';
                span.style.transform = 'translateY(10px)';
                span.style.transition = 'none';
                /* Animate to final state with per-word stagger */
                setTimeout(function() {
                  span.style.transition =
                    'opacity ' + dur + ' ' + ease +
                    ', filter ' + dur + ' ' + ease +
                    ', transform ' + dur + ' ' + ease;
                  requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                    requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                      span.style.opacity = '1';
                      span.style.filter = 'blur(0px)';
                      span.style.transform = 'translateY(0px)';
                    });
                  });
                }, startDelay + i * stagger);
              });
            }

            /* Simple opacity fade-in for an element, optional custom duration */
            function animateFade(sel, delay, customDur) {
              var el = document.querySelector(sel);
              if (!el) return;
              var d = customDur || dur;
              setTimeout(function() {
                el.style.transition = 'opacity ' + d + ' ' + ease;
                requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                  requestAnimationFrame(function() {
                    el.style.opacity = '1';
                  });
                });
              }, delay);
            }

            /* H1 heading — word by word, 70ms stagger, starts at 200ms */
            animateWords('.framer-1yft3nv h1', 200, 70);

            /* Subtitle — word by word, 70ms stagger, starts at 700ms */
            animateWords('.framer-nqkn6i p', 700, 70);

            /* CTA buttons — slow fade in at 1000ms */
            animateFade('.framer-3rv7si', 1000, '1.8s');

            /* Social proof widget (avatars + "40+ salonów") — fade in at 1100ms */
            animateFade('.framer-197f8vq-container', 1100, '1.8s');

          })();
        </script>

  <script>
    const utmKeys = ['utm_source', 'utm_medium', 'utm_campaign', 'utm_content'];
    const refKey = 'ref';
    // Store UTM and ref values from URL
    (function() {
      const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      let hasNewUTM = false;
      utmKeys.forEach(key => {
        if (urlParams.has(key)) {
          hasNewUTM = true;
        }
      });
      if (hasNewUTM) {
        utmKeys.forEach(key => {
          const value = urlParams.get(key);
          if (value) {
            localStorage.setItem(key, value);
          }
        });
      }
      if (urlParams.has(refKey)) {
        const ref = urlParams.get(refKey);
        if (ref) {
          localStorage.setItem(refKey, ref);
        }
      }
    })();

    function applyParamsToButtons() {
      const storedParams = new URLSearchParams();
      // Add UTM params from localStorage
      utmKeys.forEach(key => {
        const value = localStorage.getItem(key);
        if (value) {
          storedParams.set(key, value);
        }
      });
      // Add ref param from localStorage
      const ref = localStorage.getItem(refKey);
      if (ref) {
        storedParams.set(refKey, ref);
      }
      const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('a.buy-now');
      buttons.forEach(button => {
        try {
          const url = new URL(button.href);
          const params = new URLSearchParams(url.search);
          storedParams.forEach((value, key) => {
            params.set(key, value);
          });
          url.search = params.toString();
          button.href = url.toString();
        } catch (err) {
          console.warn('Param append error:', err);
        }
      });
    }
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', applyParamsToButtons);
    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
      applyParamsToButtons();
    });
    observer.observe(document.body, {
      childList: true,
      subtree: true
    });
  </script>
  <style>
    html,
    body {
      scroll-behavior: auto !important
    }
    /* On touch-primary devices restore smooth so native momentum + anchor links work */
    @media (pointer: coarse) {
      html,
      body {
        scroll-behavior: smooth !important
      }
      #br-cursor-dot {
        display: none !important
      }
    }
  </style>
  <script>
    (function() {
      // On touch-primary devices (phones/tablets) use native scroll — it has
      // built-in momentum and feels far better than JS lerp on those screens.
      var isTouchPrimary = window.matchMedia('(pointer: coarse)').matches;

      if (isTouchPrimary) {
        // Native scroll only. Smooth anchor links still work via scrollIntoView.
        document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
          var a = e.target.closest('a[href^="#"]');
          if (!a) return;
          var id = a.getAttribute('href').slice(1);
          var target = document.getElementById(id);
          if (!target) return;
          e.preventDefault();
          target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'start' });
        });
        return;
      }

      // Desktop / trackpad: lerp-based smooth scroll
      var SMOOTH = 0.1;
      var targetY = window.scrollY || 0;
      var currentY = targetY;
      var raf = null;
      var prevT = null;

      function maxY() {
        return Math.max(0, Math.max(document.body.scrollHeight, document.documentElement.scrollHeight) - window.innerHeight);
      }

      function setY(v) {
        try {
          window.scrollTo({ top: v, left: 0, behavior: "instant" });
        } catch (e) {
          window.scrollTo(0, v);
        }
      }

      function tick(ts) {
        if (prevT === null) prevT = ts;
        var dt = Math.min((ts - prevT) / 1000, 0.1);
        prevT = ts;
        var factor = 1 - Math.pow(1 - SMOOTH, dt * 60);
        currentY += (targetY - currentY) * factor;
        if (Math.abs(targetY - currentY) < 0.05) {
          currentY = targetY;
          setY(currentY);
          raf = null;
          prevT = null;
          return;
        }
        setY(currentY);
        raf = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
      }

      function addDelta(d) {
        targetY = Math.max(0, Math.min(maxY(), targetY + d));
        if (!raf) {
          prevT = null;
          raf = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
        }
      }

      window.addEventListener("wheel", function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var d = e.deltaY;
        if (e.deltaMode === 1) d *= 40;
        if (e.deltaMode === 2) d *= window.innerHeight;
        addDelta(d);
      }, {
        passive: false,
        capture: true
      });

      window.addEventListener("scroll", function() {
        if (raf) return;
        currentY = targetY = window.pageYOffset || window.scrollY || 0;
      }, {
        passive: true
      });

      /* Smooth-scroll anchor links */
      document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        var a = e.target.closest('a[href^="#"]');
        if (!a) return;
        var id = a.getAttribute('href').slice(1);
        var target = document.getElementById(id);
        if (!target) return;
        e.preventDefault();
        var rect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
        var scrollY = window.pageYOffset || window.scrollY || 0;
        targetY = Math.max(0, Math.min(maxY(), scrollY + rect.top - 40));
        if (!raf) {
          prevT = null;
          raf = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
        }
      });
    }());
  </script>

  <script>
    (function(){
      var burger = document.getElementById('pp-index-burger');
      var menu = document.getElementById('pp-index-mobile-menu');
      if (!burger || !menu) return;
      burger.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        var open = menu.classList.toggle('open');
        burger.classList.toggle('open', open);
        burger.setAttribute('aria-expanded', open);
      });
      document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (!burger.contains(e.target) && !menu.contains(e.target)) {
          menu.classList.remove('open');
          burger.classList.remove('open');
          burger.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
        }
      });
    })();
  </script>
